[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe timeout issue is caused by **infinite loops in Type1Parser** due to missing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull checks when consuming tokens. The fuzzer got stuck at `[0m[1;35mType1Lexer.readToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mline [0m[1;36m123[0m[39m because the parser was continuously requesting tokens in unbounded loops.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThere are **two critical locations** with identical problems:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mType1Parser.readEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m** - Loop searching for [0m[32m"dup"[0m[39m, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"readonly"[0m[39m, or [0m[32m"def"[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[39m** - Loop searching for [0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBoth loops have the same fundamental flaws:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No null checking on `[0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` before calling `[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No iteration limits to prevent unbounded execution[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Unconditional token consumption without validation[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen malformed Type1 font data causes the lexer to produce tokens that never match [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe expected keywords, these loops run indefinitely, causing the DoS timeout.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Evidence from Codebase[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase already demonstrates correct patterns:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[39m**: Properly checks `peekToken != null`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore accessing token properties[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mType1Parser.readProc[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m476[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m**: Throws IOException when [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == null`[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mType1LexerTest.readTokens[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m141[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m149[0m[39m**: Test code shows null is the EOF [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmarker[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **[0m[1;35mBaseParser.readStringNumber[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m1450[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1454[0m[39m**: Uses iteration limits [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mMAX_LENGTH_LONG[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to prevent DoS[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese patterns confirm that **null checking is the established safety mechanism** [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the Type1 parsing system.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Null Checks to Prevent Infinite Loops[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mType1Parser.readEncoding[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m223[0m[39m**[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTransform the problematic loop:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInto a safe version following the pattern from lines [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[39m:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mToken token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken != null && ![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mtoken.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mtoken.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                || [0m[1;35mtoken.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature end of file while reading encoding"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m644[0m[39m**[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTransform the problematic loop:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInto a safe version:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mToken token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken != null && ![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.LITERAL[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        && [0m[1;35mtoken.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature end of file while searching for CharStrings"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Secondary Fix: Add Iteration Limits [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDefense in Depth[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollowing the pattern from [0m[1;35mBaseParser.readStringNumber[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m1450[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1454[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstants and iteration counting as an additional safety mechanism:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd to Type1Parser class:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Maximum number of tokens to consume while searching for expected keywords[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This prevents DoS attacks through malformed fonts with excessive token sequences[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final int MAX_ENCODING_TOKENS = [0m[1;36m10000[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mEnhance both loops to include iteration counting:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mToken token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mint count = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken != null && ![0m[1;39m([0m[39mcondition[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    token = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m++count > MAX_ENCODING_TOKENS[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Too many tokens while searching for expected [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mkeyword, possible malformed font"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtoken == null[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature end of file..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Codebase Patterns**: The fix uses the exact same [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-checking pattern already present in [0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring consistency[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Minimal Code Changes**: Only modifies the two problematic loops without [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtouching the Type1Lexer or other parser logic, reducing risk of breaking existing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Backward Compatibility**: Valid Type1 fonts will continue to parse [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrectly; only malformed fonts that would cause hangs will be rejected with clear [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39merror messages[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Defense in Depth**: The combination of null checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprimary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and iteration [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlimits [0m[1;39m([0m[39msecondary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m provides robust protection against DoS attacks[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Already Proven Safe**: The null-checking pattern is demonstrated working in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple locations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m476[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m515[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m518[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the iteration limit [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern is used in BaseParser[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Prevents Infinite Loops**: Null checking ensures loops terminate when no more [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtokens are available[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Clear Error Messages**: IOException with descriptive messages help identify [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed fonts[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **DoS Prevention**: Iteration limits prevent excessive CPU consumption even if [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull checking somehow fails[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No NPE**: Checking null before calling `[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNullPointerException[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Valid but Unusual Fonts**: If legitimate fonts exist without the expected [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mkeywords, they will now throw IOException[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: The error messages clearly indicate the issue, and the [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_ENCODING_TOKENS limit of [0m[1;36m10000[0m[39m is generous enough for any legitimate use case[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Test Compatibility**: Existing tests may need updates if they use malformed [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest data[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Tests should be using valid Type1 font data; any tests that [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail were testing undefined behavior[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Performance Impact**: Adding iteration counter adds minimal overhead[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: A single integer increment per loop iteration is negligible [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompared to token parsing cost[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly mirrors:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[1;35mType1Parser.parseBinary[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m557[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m564[0m[39m**: Same null-checking pattern for token[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloops[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **[0m[1;35mBaseParser.readStringNumber[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m lines [0m[1;36m1450[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1454[0m[39m**: Same iteration limit pattern [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfor DoS prevention[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **PfbParser lines [0m[1;36m161[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m**: Size validation to prevent resource exhaustion[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix is consistent with the established security and safety patterns in PDFBox.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                   [0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=482389;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=844157;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
